#################################
######## THE FIREBEARDS #########
#################################

### In order:
#
# Line of Úri "lineofuri"
# Line of Khathzâ ibriz "khathzaibriz"
# Line of Ubraz. Guardians of the golden gate and stewards of Amak Arazi
# House of Arsan. Venerable, dying house of firebeards in the southern regions of Buzra Dum
# House of Agzay. Humble isolationists
# Line of Stone-Wall. Stalwart defenders of the gate of fire, and friends to all who come in peace
# Line of Hersar. Able captains of the Bronze guard


###############################
### Line of Úri the Scarred ###
###############################
